  patient_id INT,
  diagnosis VARCHAR(100),
  treatment VARCHAR(100),
  prescription VARCHAR(100)
);

  patient_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  patient_name VARCHAR(50),
  age INT,
  gender VARCHAR(10)
);

  appointment_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  patient_id INT,

  appointment_time TIME
